#
#   China_block

#   (주) 스마일서브 기술지원팀 김성태대리 2007-12-11
#
########################################################
#
#
# 로컬룰지정
ipsec static set store location=local

# 최초 룰정책 생성
ipsec static add policy name=China_IP_block_list activatedefaultrule=yes (주)스마일서브-중국IP리스트-차단정책 assign=yes

# 필터리스트 추가
# ipsec static add filterlist name=All
ipsec static add filterlist name=China_block
ipsec static add filterlist name=Local

# 허용/거부룰 설정
ipsec static add filteraction name=Permit action=Permit
ipsec static add filteraction name=Block action=Block

# 모든트래픽허용
# ipsec static add filter filterlist=All srcaddr=ANY dstaddr=me dstmask=255.255.255.0 protocol=ANY mirrored=yes

# 중국IP차단

ipsec static add filter filterlist=Local srcaddr=me dstaddr=localhost dstmask=255.255.255.0 protocol=ANY mirrored=yes

#  필터룰 추가
# ipsec static add rule name=2 policy=China_IP_block_list filter=All filteraction=Permit
ipsec static add rule name=3 policy=China_IP_block_list filter=China_block filteraction=Block
ipsec static add rule name=1 policy=China_IP_block_list filter=Local filteraction=Permit
